පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව பாராᾦமன்றம் PARLIAMENT —————–—-

2015 මාර්තු 13 වන සිකුරාදා 2015 மார்ச் 13, ெவள்ளிக்கிழைம Friday, 13th March, 2015 ————————— අ.භා. 3.10 ට ගණපූරණ සීනු නාද වී මන්තීවරුන් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු සභා ගර්භයට රැස් වූෙයන් - பி.ப. 3.10 க்கு, நிைறெவண் மணி அᾊத்ᾐ, உᾠப்பினர்கள் பாராᾦமன்றச் சபாமண்டபத்திற் கூᾊயᾐம் - The Quorum Bells having been rung at 3.10 p.m., and Members having assembled in the Chamber of Parliament -

අ.භා. 3.15ට කථානායකතුමා [ගරු චමල් රාජපක්ෂ මහතා] ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමා සමඟ පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු සභා ගර්භයට ඇතුළු විය.

කථානායකතුමා මූලාසනාරූඪ විය.

ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමා කථානායකතුමා අසලින් වූ අසුෙනහි වාඩි වූෙය්ය.

பி.ப. 3.15 க்கு, சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள் [மாண்ᾗமிகு சமல் ராஜபக்ஷ] இந்தியப் பிரதம அைமச்சரான ேமதகு ஸ்ரீ நேரந்திர ேமாᾊ அவர்கᾦடன் பாராᾦமன்றச் சபாமண்டபத்ᾐட் பிரேவசித்தார்கள்.

சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள் அக்கிராசனத்தமர்ந்தார்கள்.

ேமதகு ஸ்ரீ நேரந்திர ேமாᾊ சபாநாயகர் மᾞங்கிᾢᾞந்த ஆசனத்தமர்ந்தார்கள்.

Mr. Speaker [The Hon. Chamal Rajapaksa] with His Excellency Shri Narendra Modi, Prime Minister of India, entered the Chamber at 3.15 p.m.

Mr. Speaker took the Chair. His Excellency Shri Narendra Modi took his seat beside Mr. Speaker.

කථානායකතුමා (சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (Mr. Speaker) Your Excellency Shri Narendra Modi, Prime Minister of India, Hon. Prime Minister of Sri Lanka, Hon. Leader of the Opposition, Hon. Ministers, Hon. Members of Parliament, Excellencies, Distinguished Invitees, I am deeply honoured and privileged to welcome Your Excellency to the Parliament of Sri Lanka on your historic and momentous visit.

It is noteworthy that a visit by a Prime Minister of India to Sri Lanka is taking place after 28 years. Your Excellency's visit to this Parliament and your Address to the Hon. Members has an added honour and significance because you are the first Indian Prime Minister to address a session of Parliament.

Our countries and people have had centuries-old relationship through common cultural, religious and civilizational bonds. The deeply cherished traditions of Buddhism and Hinduism prosper amongst our peoples. Today, our countries share an all-encompassing development partnership through our common cultural and religious contacts, vibrant economic engagement, and security interests.

Your Excellency, India and Sri Lanka have democratic traditions and democratic institutions that are

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු විවාද

නිල වාර්තාව ශී ලංකා පජාතාන්තික සමාජවාදී ජනරජ ය හත්වන පාර්ලි ෙම්න් තුව - පළමුවන සභා වාරය

பாராᾦமன்ற விவாதங்கள்

அதிகார அறிக்ைக இலங்ைகச் சனநாயக ேசாசᾢசக் குᾊயரசின் ஏழாவᾐ பாராᾦமன்றம் - ᾙதலாவᾐ கூட்டத் ெதாடர்

PARLIAMENTARY DEBATES OFFICIAL REPORT THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA SEVENTH PARLIAMENT - FIRST SESSION

233 වන කාණ්ඩය ெதாகுதி 233 VOLUME 233

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

more than half a century old. The Indian General Election may probably be considered as the greatest democratic exercise of the world. We can also be proud that we have practised, sustained, and nurtured democracy in its true spirit for several centuries. The existence of democratic concepts, as practised by Licchavi rulers, is also manifested in our history.

At this time of opportune, let me recall the history of relationship between our two Legislatures. The India-Sri Lanka Parliamentary Friendship Association was formally inaugurated in December 2005. Since then, delegations from both Parliamentary Friendship Associations have paid reciprocal visits. The most recent visit to our Parliament from India was by the Hon. Sushma Swaraj and the delegation in April, 2012. I have noted that even before the formal establishment of the Association, our Parliamentarians have been visiting each other.

Today, I am happy to note that I am one of the Patrons of the India-Sri Lanka Parliamentary Friendship Association and the Hon. Leader of the Opposition of this House is the President of it. It is heartening to note that the membership of the Association cut across the party lines. The visits by our Parliamentarians of both countries are important milestones in our relations which contribute to a better understanding between our countries and its peoples. In this connection, I am happy to recall the State Visit of His Excellency President Maithripala Sirisena to India last month.

Your Excellency, on the 26th of May, last year, you took Oath as the Prime Minister of India after receiving a resounding mandate from your people. Before that, during your 13-year-long stint as the Chief Minister of Gujarat, you transformed the State into a growth engine.

Your achievements as the Chief Minister of Gujarat are legendary and, in fact, the model you followed in developing Gujarat is an inspiration to many. You started your career as a politician in your late teens. You have risen through the ranks of BJP through sheer hard work, dedication and determination which culminated in your ascendancy as the Prime Minister of India. I am confident that Your Excellency’s visit to this Legislature and your words of wisdom will immensely contribute to further cement the relations between us.

Your Excellency, on behalf of the Parliament of Sri Lanka, may I wish you good health, happiness and may your visit to this country be a memorable one for both our nations.

Now, let me have the privilege and honour to invite His Excellency Shri Narendra Modi, Prime Minister of India, to deliver his Address.

ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමාෙග් ෙද්ශනය இந்தியப் பிரதம அைமச்சர் ேமதகு ஸ்ரீ நேரந்திர ேமாᾊ அவர்களᾐ உைர ADDRESS BY HIS EXCELLENCY SHRI NARENDRA MODI, PRIME MINISTER OF INDIA ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමා (ேமதகு ஸ்ரீ நேரந்திர ேமாᾊ - இந்தியப் பிரதம அைமச்சர்) (His Excellency Shri Narendra Modi - Prime Minister of India) Hon. Speaker of Parliament, Shrimaan Chamal Rajapaksa ji, Hon. Prime Minister of Sri Lanka, Shrimaan Ranil Wickremasinghe ji, Hon. Leader of the Opposition, Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva, Hon. Members of Parliament, and Distinguished Guests. I am truly delighted to visit Sri Lanka, a land of beauty, culture and friendship. I am deeply honoured to be in this Parliament. I am conscious of its rich history. This Parliament represents one of Asia's oldest democracies and one of its most vibrant. Long before many others in the world, Sri Lanka gave every individual a vote and voice.

To the people of Sri Lanka, Ayubowan! Vanakkam! I bring the greetings of 1.25 billion friends and millions of fans of Sri Lankan cricket. I bring the blessings from the land of Bodh Gaya to the land of Anuradhapura. I stand here with respect for our shared heritage and with commitment to our shared future. Last May, when I took the Oath of office, I was honoured by the presence of South Asian leaders at the ceremony. Their presence was a celebration of democracy's march forward in our region. It was also recognition of our common destiny. I am convinced that the future of any country is influenced by the state of its neighbourhood. The future that I dream for India is also the future that I wish for our neighbours. We, in this region, are on the same journey: to transform the lives of our people.

Our path will be easier, the journey quicker and the destination nearer, when we walk step in step. As I stand here in Colombo and look north towards the Himalaya, I marvel at our region's uniqueness - of our rich diversity and common civilizational links. We have been formed from the same elements and from our interconnected histories. Today, we stand together as proud, independent nations, sovereign and equal. India and Sri Lanka do not have a land boundary, but we are the closest neighbours in every sense. No matter where you look in India or Sri Lanka, the many strands of our links - religions, languages, cultures, foods, customs, traditions and epics - come together into a deep and strong bond of familiarity and friendship. Ours is a relationship that is beautifully defined by the journey of Mahendra and Sanghamitra. They carried the message of peace, tolerance and friendship more than two millenniums ago. It is evoked by Kannagi, the central character of the great Tamil epic Silapathikaram, who is worshipped as Goddess the Pattini

3 4

[කථානායකතුමා]

2015 මාර්තු 13

in Sri Lanka; it lives in the Ramayan trail in Sri Lanka; it expresses itself in devotion at the Dargah of the Nagore Andavar and the Christian shrine of Velankanni; it is reflected in the friendship of Swami Vivekananda and Anagarika Dharmapala, the founder of the Maha Bodhi Society in Sri Lanka and India and it lives in the work of Mahatma Gandhi's followers in India and Sri Lanka. Above all, our relationship thrives through the interwoven lives of ordinary Indians and Sri Lankans. Our independent life began at about the same time. Sri Lanka has made remarkable progress since then.

The nation is an inspiration for our region in human development. Sri Lanka is home to enterprise, skill and extraordinary intellectual heritage. There are businesses of global class here. Sri Lanka is a leader in advancing cooperation in South Asia and it is important for the future of the Indian Ocean Region. Sri Lanka's progress and prosperity are also a source of strength for India. So, Sri Lanka's success is of great significance to India and as a friend, our good wishes, our support and solidarity have always been with Sri Lanka and it will always be there for you. For all of us in our region, our success depends on how we define ourselves as a nation. All of us in this region, indeed every nation of diversity, have dealt with the issues of identities and inclusion, rights and claims, dignity and opportunity for different sections of our societies. We all have seen its diverse expressions. We have faced tragic violence; we have encountered brutal terrorism and we have also seen successful examples of peaceful settlements. Each of us has sought to address these complex issues in our own way. However, we choose to reconcile them. To me, something is obvious: diversity can be a source of strength for nations.

When we accommodate the aspirations of all sections of our society, the nation gets the strength of every individual. And, when we empower states, districts and villages, we make our country stronger and stronger. You can call this, my bias. I have been a Chief Minister for 13 years; a Prime Minister, for less than a year!

Today, my top priority is to make the States in India stronger. I am a firm believer in cooperative federalism. So, we are devolving more power and more resources to the States and we are making them formal partners in national decision- making processes.

Sri Lanka has lived through decades of tragic violence and conflict. You have successfully defeated terrorism and brought the conflict to an end. You now stand at a moment of historic opportunity to win the hearts and heal the wounds across all sections of society. Recent elections in Sri Lanka have reflected the collective voice of the nation: the hope for change, reconciliation and unity. The steps that you have taken in recent times are bold and admirable. They represent a new beginning.

I am confident of a future for Sri Lanka defined by unity and integrity, peace and harmony and opportunity and dignity for everyone. I believe in Sri Lanka’s ability to achieve it. It is rooted in our common civilizational heritage. The path ahead is a choice that Sri Lanka has to make and it is a collective responsibility of all sections of the society and of all political streams in the country. But, I can assure you of this: for India, the unity and integrity of Sri Lanka are paramount. It is rooted in our interest. It stems from our own fundamental beliefs in this principle.

Hon. Speaker and Distinguished Members, my vision of an ideal neighbourhood is one in which trade, investments, technology, ideas and people flow easily across borders, when partnerships in the region are formed with the ease of routine.

In India, the growth momentum has been restored. India has become the fastest growing major economy in the world. The world sees India as the new frontier of economic opportunity. But, our neighbours should have the first claim on India. And I again repeat, the first claim on India is of our neighbours, of Sri Lanka. I will be happy if India serves as a catalyst in the progress of our neighbours. In our region, Sri Lanka has the potential to be our strongest economic partner. We will work with you to address your concerns to boost trade and make it more balanced. India's trade environment is becoming more and more open. Sri Lanka should not fall behind others in this competitive world. That is why we should conclude an ambitious Comprehensive Economic Partnership Agreement. India can also be a natural source of investments for exports to India and elsewhere and to build your infrastructure. We have made good progress today. Let us work together to harness the vast potential of the Ocean Economy.

Our two nations must also take the lead in increasing cooperation in the South Asian Region and the linked BIMSTEC Region. Connecting this vast region by land and sea, our two countries can become engines of regional prosperity. I also assure you of India's full commitment to development partnership with Sri Lanka. We see this as a responsibility of a friend and a neighbour. India has committed US Dollars 1.6 billion in development assistance. Today, we have committed further assistance up to US Dollars 318 million to the railway sector. We will continue our development partnership. We will be guided by your Government. And, we will do so with the same level of transparency that we expect in our own country. Last month, we signed the agreement on cooperation in peaceful uses of nuclear energy. More than anywhere else in the region, I see enormous potential to expand cooperation with Sri Lanka in areas like agriculture, education, health, science and technology, and space.

Indeed, we are limited only by our imagination. We hope that Sri Lanka will take full benefit of India's

5 6

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

satellite for the SAARC Region. This should be in space by December 2016. People are at the heart of our relationship. When we connect people, bonds between nations become stronger. That is why we have decided to extend the Visa-on-Arrival facility to Sri Lankan citizens. We will also increase connectivity between our countries. We will strengthen ties of culture and religion. Last month, we announced reduction in fees for Sri Lankan nationals visiting National Museum in Delhi to see the Kapilavastu Relics. We will bring our shared Buddhist heritage closer to you through an exhibition. Together, we will develop our Buddhist and Ramayana Trails. My birth place Varnagarh was an international centre of Buddhist learning in ancient times. Excavations have revealed a hostel for 2000 students and in plans to redevelop the centre.

Hon. Speaker, a future of prosperity requires a strong foundation of security for our countries and peace and stability in the region. The security of our two countries is indivisible. Equally, our shared responsibility for our maritime neighbourhood is clear. India and Sri Lanka are too close to look away from each other, nor can we be insulated from one another. Our recent histories have shown that we suffer together; and we are more effective when we work with each other. Our cooperation helped deal with the devastation of tsunami in 2004. As a Chief Minister, I was pleased to share our experience in reconstruction after the Bhuj earthquake in 2001. Our cooperation is also integral to our success in combating terrorism and extremism.

For both of us, local threats remain. But, we see threats arising in new forms and from new sources. We are witnessing globalization of terrorism. The need for our cooperation has never been stronger than today. The Indian Ocean is critical to the security and prosperity of our two countries. And, we can be more successful in achieving these goals if we work together, build a climate of trust and confidence, and remain sensitive to each other's interest. We deeply value our security cooperation with Sri Lanka. We should expand the maritime security cooperation between India, Sri Lanka and Maldives to include others in the Indian Ocean area.

I often say that the course of the 21st Century would be determined by the currents of the Indian Ocean. Shaping its direction is a responsibility for the countries in the region. We are two countries at the crossroads of the Indian Ocean. Your leadership and our partnership will be vital for building a peaceful, secure, stable and prosperous maritime neighbourhood. In our deeply interconnected lives, it is natural to have differences. Sometimes, it touches the lives of the ordinary people. We have the openness in our dialogue, the strength of our human values and, the goodwill in our relationship to resolve them.

Hon. Speaker, Sri Lanka and India are at a moment of a great opportunity and responsibility - for realizing the dreams of our people. This is also a time for renewal in our relationship; for a new beginning and new vigour in our partnership. We have to ensure that our proximity always translates into closeness. We were honoured that President Sirisena chose India as his first destination last month. I am honoured to be his first guest here. This is how it should be between neighbours. Tomorrow, I will go to Talaimannar to flag off the train to Madhu Road. This is part of the old India - Lanka rail link. I recall the lines of a famous song "Sindu Nadiyin Misai" composed by the great nationalist poet Subramanian Bharati in the early 20th Century: ‘Singala theevunukkoor paalam ameippom’ - we shall construct a bridge to Sri Lanka.

I have come with the hope of building this bridge - a bridge that rests on strong pillars of our shared inheritance; of shared values and vision; of mutual support and solidarity; of friendly exchanges and productive cooperation; and, above all, belief in each other and our shared destiny.

Thank you, it is an honour to have been with you. Thank you very much, once again.

කථාෙව් සිංහල පරිවර්තනය உைரயினᾐ சிங்கள ெமாழிெபயர்ப்ᾗ SINHALA TRANSLATION OF THE SPEECH

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු ෙව් ගරු කථානායක ශීමාන් චමල් රාජපක්ෂ මැතිතුමනි, ශී ලංකාෙව් ගරු අගාමාත්‍ය ශීමාන් රනිල් විකමසිංහ මැතිතුමනි, ගරු විරුද්ධ පාර්ශ්වෙය් නායක නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මැතිතුමනි, ගරු පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු මන්තීවරුනි, සම්භාවනීය අමුත්තනි, සුන්දරත්වෙයන්, සංස්කෘතිෙයන් හා සුහදත්වෙයන් සපිරි ශී ලංකා ෙද්ශෙයහි සංචාරය කිරීමට මා හට අවස්ථාව ලැබීම පිළිබඳව මම සැබවින්ම සතුටට පත් ෙවමි. මට ෙමම පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුවට පැමිණීම ඉමහත් ෙගෞරවයකි. මම ෙමහි ෙපෞඪ ඉතිහාසය පිළිබඳව දනිමි. ෙමම පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ආසියාෙව් පැරණිතම පජාතන්තයන්ෙගන් එකක් හා වඩාත් කියාශීලී ඒවායින් එකක් නිෙයෝජනය කරයි. ශී ලංකාව, සෑම තැනැත්තකුටම ඡන්දයක් හා හඬක් ලබා දුන්ෙන් ෙලෝකෙය් ෙසේසසන් ෙබොෙහෝ ෙදනකුට ෙපර ය.

ශී ලංකාෙව් ජනතාවට ආයුෙබෝවන්, වනක්කම්! මම මිතුරන් ෙකෝටි 12 ½කෙගන් සහ ශී ලංකා කිකට් කණ්ඩායම් ෙලෝලීන් ලක්ෂ ගණනකෙගන් සුභ පැතුම් රැෙගන පැමිණිෙයමි. මම බුද්ධගයාව ෙද්ශෙය් සිට අනුරාධපුර ෙද්ශය ෙවත ආශිර්වාද රැෙගන පැමිණිෙයමි. මම ෙමහි නැගී සිටිනුෙය් අපෙග් හවුල් උරුමය ෙකෙරහි ගරුත්වය හා අපෙග් හවුල් අනාගතය ෙකෙරහි ඇපකැප වීම ඇතිව ය. මම පසුගිය මැයි මාසෙය් දිවුරුම් ෙදන අවස්ථාෙව්දී, එම උත්සවයට ආසියාතික නායකයින් සහභාගී වීම මට ෙගෞරවයක් විය. ඔවුන්ෙග් සහභාගිත්වය අපෙග් කලාපය තුළ පජාතන්තවාදෙය් ඉදිරි ගමන සැමරීමක් විය. එෙමන්ම එය අපෙග් ඉරණම හවුල් ඉරණමක් බව පිළිගැනීමක් ද විය. කවර රටක වුවද අනාගතය ෙකෙරහි එහි අසල්වැසියන්ෙග් තත්ත්වය බලපාන බව මට ඒත්තු ෙගොස් තිෙබ්. මම ඉන්දියාව ෙවනුෙවන් සිහින මවන අනාගතය, අපෙග් අසල්වැසියන් ෙවනුෙවන් මා පාර්ථනා කරන අනාගතය ද ෙවයි. ෙමම කලාපෙයහි අපි එකම ගමෙනහි, අපෙග් ජනතාවෙග් ජීවිත විපරිණාමනය කිරීෙම් ගමෙනහි, ෙයදී සිටිමු.

අපෙග් මග වඩාත් පහසු, ගමන වඩාත් ඉක්මන් හා ගමනාන්තය වඩාත් ළං ළං වනු ඇත්ෙත් අපි පියවෙරන් පියවර පිය නගන විට ය. මම ෙමෙසේ ෙකොළඹ සිටෙගන හිමාලය ෙදස බලන විට, අප කලාපෙය්

7 8

[ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමා]

2015 මාර්තු 13

සුවිෙශේෂී අනන්‍යතාවය, එනම් අපෙග් විවිධත්වෙයහි හා ෙපොදු ශිෂ්ටාචාරමය සම්බන්ධතාවන්හි සුවිෙශේෂී අනන්‍යතාවය පිළිබඳව මම මවිත ෙවමි. අප සෑදී ඇත්ෙත් එකම ෙපොදු මූලයන්ෙගන් හා අපෙග් එකිෙනකට බද්ධ වූ ඉතිහාසයන්ෙගන් ය. අද අපි අභිමානවත්, ස්වාධීන රාජ්‍යයන් වශෙයන් ස්ෛවරීව හා සමානව එකට නැඟී සිටිමු. ඉන්දියාව හා ශී ලංකාව අතර භූමි සම්බන්ධයක් ෙනොමැති වුව ද, අපි වචනෙය් පරිසමාප්ත අර්ථෙයන්ම සමීපතම අසල්වැසිෙයෝ ෙවමු. ඔබ ෙනත් ෙයොමන්ෙන් ඉන්දියාෙව් හා ශී ලංකාෙව් ෙකොතැනට වුවත්, අපෙග් සබඳකම්වල බහුවිධ පුරුක් - ආගම්, භාෂා, සංස්කෘති, ආහාරපාන, චාරිත වාරිත, සම්පදායන් හා වීරකාව්‍ය - එකට එක්ව ගැඹුරු හා ශක්තිමත් සමීපත්වෙය් හා සුහදත්වෙය් බැඳීමක් ඇති කරයි. අපෙග් බැඳීම මාෙහේන්ද හා සංඝමිතෙග් ආගමනෙයන් විචිත ෙලස ඔප් නැංවුණු බැඳීමකි. ඔවුහු සාමෙය්, උෙප්ක්ෂාෙව් හා මිතත්වෙය් පණිවුඩය රැෙගන ආෙව් සහස ෙදකකටත් ෙපරදීම ය. ශී ලංකාව් පත්තිනි ෙද්විය ෙලස බුහුමන් ලබන ෙදමළ මහා කාව්‍ය වන සිලප්පතිකාරම්හි පධාන චරිතය වන කන්නගී විසින් ද ෙමය මතු කර තිෙබනවා; ශී ලංකාෙව් රාමායණ කථාෙව් ද එය ජීවත් ෙවනවා; නාෙගෝර් අන්දවාර් හි දර්ගා හි ද, ෙව්ලක්කන්නිහි තිෙබන කිස්තියානි සිද්ධස්ථානෙය් ද භක්තිෙයන් යුතුව එය පකාශ ෙවනවා; ස්වාමි විෙව්කානන්ද සහ ශී ලංකාෙව් සහ ඉන්දියාෙව් මහා ෙබෝධි සමාගෙම් නිර්මාතෘ වන අනගාරික ධර්මපාලතුමා අතර පැවති මිතත්වෙය් ද ඉන්දියාෙව් සහ ශී ලංකාෙව් මහත්මා ගාන්ධිතුමාෙග් අනුගාමිකයන් ෙග් කියාකාරකම් තුළ ද එය ජීවත් ෙවනවා. ඒ සියල්ලටම වඩා අපෙග් සබඳතාව ශක්තිමත්ව වැෙඩන්ෙන් ඉන්දියාෙව් සහ ශී ලංකාෙව් ෙවෙසන සාමාන්‍ය ජනතාවෙග් එකට බැඳුන ජීවිත හරහායි. අපෙග් නිදහස් ජීවිතය ආරම්භ වන්ෙන් ද එකම කාලයක ය. එදා පටන් ශී ලංකාව සැලකිය යුතු පගතියක් ලබා තිෙබනවා.

ෙමම රට මානව සංවර්ධනය සම්බන්ධෙයන් ගත් විට අපෙග් කලාපය තුළ නව පිබිදීමක් ඇති කිරීමට සමත් වී තිෙබනවා. ශී ලංකාව, ව්‍යවසායන්, නිපුණතාවන් සහ අසාමාන්‍ය බුද්ධිමය උරුමයන්ට නිවහනකි. ෙමහි ෙගෝලීය මට්ටෙම් ව්‍යාපාර තිෙබනවා. දකුණු ආසියාෙව් ඉදිරියට යන සහෙයෝගිතාෙව් ශී ලංකාව ෙපරමුෙණ් සිටින රටක් වන අතර, ඉන්දීය සාගර කලාපෙය් අනාගතයට එය ඉතාමත් වැදගත් ෙවනවා. ශී ලංකාෙව් දියුණුව සහ සමෘද්ධිය ඉන්දියාවට ශක්තිමත් මූලාශයක් සපයනවා. එම නිසා ශී ලංකාෙව් සාර්ථකත්වය ඉන්දියාවට විෙශේෂ වැදගත් කාරණයක් වනවා. ශී ලංකාෙව් මිතුෙරක් වශෙයන් ඉන්දියාෙව් ශුභාසිංශන, සහාය සහ සහෙයෝගිතාව සෑම විටම ශී ලංකාව සමඟ වන අතර, එය සෑම විටම ඔබ ෙවනුෙවන් ඒ ආකාරෙයන්ම පවතිනු ඇත. අප කලාපෙය් සිටින සියලු ෙදනා සඳහා අපෙග් සාර්ථකත්වය තීරණය වන්ෙන් අප ජාතියක් වශෙයන් අපව නිර්වචනය කර ගන්නා ආකාරය අනුවයි. ෙමම කලාපෙය් සිටින සියලුෙදනා, ඇත්ත වශෙයන්ම විවිධත්වය සහිත ජාතීන් තුළ සමාජෙය් විවිධ අංශ සම්බන්ධෙයන් අනන්‍යතාවන් සහ අන්තර්ගත කිරීම්, අයිතිවාසිකම් සහ හිමිකම්, අභිමානය සහ අවස්ථාවන් සම්බන්ධ ගැටලුවලට මුහුණ දී තිෙබනවා. එහි විවිධ වූ පකාශන අප සියලුෙදනා දැක තිෙබනවා. අප ෙඛ්දනීය පචණ්ඩත්වයන්ට මුහුණ දී තිෙබනවා; අප, අතිශය දරුණු තස්තවාදය අත් දැක තිෙබනවා ෙමන්ම සාමකාමී ෙලස නිරවුල් වූ සාර්ථක උදාහරණත් අප දැක තිෙබනවා. ෙමම සංකීර්ණ ගැටලු විසඳා ගැනීමට අෙප්ම කමයක් ෙසොයා ගැනීමට අපට අවශ්‍ය ෙවනවා. ෙකෙසේ ෙවතත් ඔවුන් සමඟ සමාදාන වීම අප ෙතෝරා ගත යුතුයි. මට එක් ෙදයක් පැහැදිලියි. විවිධත්වය ජාතියකට ශක්තිෙය් මූලාශයක් විය හැකියි.

අප සමාජෙය් සියලුම අංශවල අෙප්ක්ෂාවන් සලකා බැලු විට සෑම පුද්ගලෙයකුෙග්ම ශක්තිය මඟින් ජාතිය ෙපොෙහොසත් වීම සිදු ෙවනවා. එෙසේම අප පාන්ත, දිස්තික්ක සහ ගම් බලගැන්වූ විට අෙප් රට තව තවත් ශක්තිමත් ෙවනවා. ෙමය මෙග් පක්ෂපාතිත්වය ෙලස ඔබට සිතන්නට හැකියාව තිෙබනවා. මම මහ ඇමතිවරෙයක් වශෙයන් වසර 13 ක් ෙසේවය කළත් අගමැතිවරෙයක් වශෙයන් ෙසේවය කර ඇත්ෙත් වසරකට අඩු කාලයකුයි.

අද මා ඉහළම පමුඛත්වය ලබා දී තිෙබන්ෙන් ඉන්දියාෙව් තිෙබන පාන්ත වඩාත් ශක්තිමත් කිරීමටයි. මා සහෙයෝගී සන්ධීය කමය පිළිබඳ දැඩි ෙලස විශ්වාස කරනවා. එම නිසා අප පාන්තවලට වැඩි වශෙයන් බලතල ලබා ෙදන අතර ජාතික තීරණ ගැනීෙම් කියාවලිෙය්දී අපි ඔවුන්ව විධිමත් පාර්ශ්වකරුවන් කර ගන්නවා.

ශී ලංකාව දශක ගණනාවක් පුරා ෙඛ්දජනක පචණ්ඩත්වෙය් සහ අර්බුදවලට මුහුණ පා තිෙබනවා. ඔබට සාර්ථක ෙලස තස්තවාදය පරාජය

ෙකොට ගැටුම් අවසන් කිරීමට හැකිවී තිෙබනවා. දැන් ඔබ සිටින්ෙන් සමාජෙය් සියලුම අංශවල සිත් දිනා ගැනීම සහ තුවාල සුව කිරීමට ලැබී ඇති ඓතිහාසික අවස්ථාවකයි. ශී ලංකාෙව් මෑතක පැවැත්වූ ඡන්දය ජනතාවෙග් සාමුහික හඬ; ෙවනසක් සඳහා වූ බලාෙපොෙරොත්තුව, පතිසන්ධානය සහ එකමුතු බව පැහැදිලිව නිරූපණය කරනවා. මෑත කාලය තුළ ඔබ ගත් පියවර නිර්භීත ෙමන්ම අගය කළ යුතු තත්ත්වයක තිෙබනවා. ඒවා නව ආරම්භයක් සනිටුහන් කරයි.

අනාගත ශී ලංකාව තුළ එක්සත් බව හා ඒකීයභාවය, සාමය හා සමඟිය සහ සෑම පුද්ගලයකුහටම අවස්ථාවන් හා අභිමානය අර්ථ ගන්වනු ඇතැයි මම විශ්වාස කරමි. එකී තත්ත්වය අත් පත් කර ගැනීමට ශී ලංකාවට හැකියාව ඇතැයි මම විශ්වාස කරමි. එය අපෙග් ෙපොදු ශිෂ්ටාචාර උරුමය තුළ මුල් බැසෙගන ඇත. ඉදිරි මඟ කවරක්ද යන්න ශී ලංකාව විසින් ෙතෝරා ගත යුතු අතර එය සමාජෙය් සියලුම අංශ සහ රෙටහි සියලුම ෙද්ශපාලන පවාහයන්ෙග් සාමූහික වගකීමක් ෙව්. ෙකෙසේ වුවද, ශී ලංකාෙව් එක්සත් බව හා ඒකීය භාවය ඉන්දියාව විසින් අතɖත්කෘෂ්ට ෙලස සලකන බව ඔබ සැමට සහතික ෙලස පකාශ කිරීමට මම කැමැත්ෙතමි. අපෙග් ළබැඳියාව තුළ එය මුල් බැස ෙගන ඇත. ෙමම පතිපත්තිය පිළිබඳ අපෙග් මූලික විශ්වාසයන්ෙග් පතිඵලයක් ෙලස එය හැඳින්විය හැකිය.

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, සම්භාවනීය මන්තීවරුනි, පරමාදර්ශී අසල්වැසිභාවය යනුෙවන් මාදකිනුෙය්, ෙවළඳාම, ආ ෙයෝජන, තාක්ෂණය, අදහස් හා ජනතාව පහසුෙවන් ෙද්ශ සීමා හරහා ගමන් කරනු ලබන, නිතිපතා පහසුෙවන් කලාපීය සහෙයෝගීතාවයන් ෙගොඩ නැගීමට අවස්ථාවන් සහිත, එකක් බවයි.

ඉන්දියාෙව් ආර්ථික වර්ධන ෙව්ගය පතිෂ්ඨාපනය කරනු ලැබ ඇත. ෙලෝකෙයහි ෙව්ගෙයන්ම වර්ධනය වන ආර්ථිකය බවට ඉන්දියානු ආර්ථිකය පත්ව ඇත. ෙලෝකය විසින් ඉන්දියාව දකිනුෙය් නව ආර්ථික අවස්ථාවන්ෙග් නව ඉමක් ෙලසය. ෙකෙසේවුවද ඉන්දියාව පිළිබඳ පළමු අයිතිවාසිකම තිබිය යුත්ෙත් අපෙග් අසල්වැසියන්හටය. එෙලසම අපෙග් අසල්වැසියකු වන ශී ලංකාවට ඉන්දියාව පිළිබඳ පළමු අයිතිවාසිකම ඇති බව නැවත වතාවක් පකාශ කිරීමට මම කැමැත්ෙතමි. අපෙග් අසල්වැසියන්ෙග් අභිවෘද්ධිය වර්ධනය කරනු ලබන සාධකයක් ෙලස ඉන්දියාවට කියා කළ හැකි නම් මම සතුටු ෙවමි. අපෙග් කලාපය තුළ අපෙග් පබලතම ආර්ථික සහකරු බවට පත්වීෙම් හැකියාව ශී ලංකාව සතුව ඇත. ෙවළඳාම පවර්ධනය කිරීම හා එය වඩාත් සමතුලිත මට්ටමකට ෙගන ඒම සඳහා ඔබ දක්වන උනන්දුව පිළිබඳව ඔබ සමඟ කටයුතු කිරීමට අපි කැමැත්ෙතමු. ඉන්දියාෙව් ෙව ළඳ පරිසරය වඩ වඩාත් විවෘත ෙවමින් පවතී. ෙමම තරගකාරී ෙලෝකය තුළ අන් අය පිටුපසින් ශී ලංකාව ගමන් කළ යුතු නැත. මහත් අෙප්ක්ෂාවන්ෙගන් සපිරි විස්තීර්ණ ආර්ථික සහෙයෝගීතා ගිවිසුමක් පිළිබඳ තීරණයකට අප එළඹිය යුත්ෙත් එබැවිනි. ඉන්දියාවට සහ ඉන් ඔබ්බට සිදු කරනු ලබන අපනයනයන් සඳහා අව්‍යාජ අෙයෝජන පභවයක් වීමට සහ ඔබෙග් යටිතල පහසුකම් ෙගොඩනැගීමට ඉන්දියාවට හැකියාව ඇත. අද අපි ඉතා ෙහොඳ පගතියක් ලබා ඇත්ෙතමු. සමුදික ආර්ථිකෙයහි සුවිශාල ශක්‍යතාවන් අත්පත්කර ගැනීමට අපි එක්ව කටයුතු කරමු.

දකුණු ආසියානු කලාපය තුළ සහ “බිම්ස්ෙටක්” කලාපීය රටවල් සමූහය සමඟ සහෙයෝගීතාවය වැඩිදියුණු කර ගැනීම සඳහා ද අප ජාතීන් ෙදක ෙපරමුණ ගත යුතුය. ෙමම සුවිසල් කලාපය ෙගොඩබිමින් හා මුහුදින් සම්බන්ධ කරමින් කලාපීය සමෘද්ධිෙයහි නියමුවන් බවට පත්වීමට අප ෙදරටට හැකියාව ඇත. ශී ලංකාෙවහි සංවර්ධන හවුල්කරු වකු බවට පත් වීමට ඉන්දියාව පූර්ණ වශෙයන් කැප වන බවට මම සහතික ෙවමි. මිතුරකුෙග් හා අසල්වැසියකුෙග් වගකීමක් ෙලස අපි ෙමය දකිමු. ඉන්දියාව විසින් ඇ.ෙඩො. බිලියන1.6ක් සංවර්ධන ආධාර ෙලස ලබා දී ඇත. දුම්රිය අංශය සඳහා ඇ.ෙඩො. මිලියන 318 දක්වා වන වැඩිදුර ආධාර අද අපි ලබා දී ඇත්ෙතමු. අපෙග් සංවර්ධන සහෙයෝගීතාවය අඛණ්ඩව පවත්වා ෙගන යාමට අපි කටයුතු කරමු. ඔබෙග් රජය විසින් අපහට මඟ ෙපන්වා ෙදනු ඇත. එෙලසම අපෙග් රටතුළ අප බලාෙපොෙරොත්තු වන මට්ටෙම්ම පාරදෘශ්‍යභාවයක් තබා ගනිමින් අපි එම කාර්යය සිදු කරමු.

න්‍යෂ්ටික ශක්තිෙයහි සාමකාමී පරිහරණයන් පිළිබඳ සහෙයෝගීතා ගිවිසුම පසුගිය මාසෙය්දී අපි අත්සන් කෙළමු. කෘෂිකර්මය, අධ්‍යාපනය, ෙසෞඛ්‍යය, විද්‍යාව හා තාක්ෂණය සහ අභ්‍යවකාශය යන ක්ෙෂේත තුළ ශී ලංකාව සමඟ සහෙයෝගීතාවය පුළුල් කිරීෙම්දී කලාපෙයහි අන් කවර ස්ථානයකටත් වඩා වැඩි ශක්‍යතාවයක් ඇති බව මම දකිමි.

9 10

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

සැබවින්ම අපහට සීමා මායිම් ෙයොදනුෙය් අපෙග් පරිකල්පනය මඟින් පමණි. “සාර්ක්” කලාපය සඳහා වන ඉන්දියානු චන්දිකාවලින් ශී ලංකාව පූර්ණ පතිලාභ අත්කර ගනු ඇතැයි අපි අෙප්ක්ෂා කරමු. 2016 ෙදසැම්බර් වන විට ෙමය අභ්‍යාවකාශ ගත කළ යුතුයි. මිනිසුන් අපෙග් සම්බන්ධතාවෙය් වැදගත්ම ෙකොටසයි. අප විසින් මිනිසුන් සම්බන්ධ කරන විට ජාතීන් අතර බැඳීම් වඩාත් ශක්තිමත් ෙවනවා. ශී ලාංකික පුරවැසියන්ට රටට පැමිණ වීසා ලබා ගැනීෙම් පහසුව -Visa -on- Arrival- ලබා ෙදන්නට අප තීරණය කර තිෙබන්ෙන් ඒ නිසයි. අප සියලුෙදනාම විසින් අපෙග් රටවල් අතර සම්බන්ධතාවයත් වර්ධනය කර ගනිමු. සංස්කෘතිය හා ආගම සම්බන්ධ බැඳීම් අප ශක්තිමත් කර ගන්න ඕන ෙවනවා. කපිලවස්තු ධාතූන් වහන්ෙසේලා බලන්නට දිල්ලි ජාතික ෙකෞතුකාගාරය ෙවත එන ශී ලාංකිකයන්ෙගන් අය කරන ගාස්තු අඩු කරන්නට අපි පසු ගිය මාසෙය්දී නිෙව්දනය කළා. අප ෙදපාර්ශවයටම ෙපොදු ෙබෞද්ධ උරුමය පදර්ශනයක් මඟින් ඔබ සමීයට ෙගන එන්නට අප කටයුතු කරනවා. ඒ සමඟම අපි අපෙග් ෙබෞද්ධ හා රාමායනය පියමං සළකුණු වර්ධනය කර ගනිමු. මා උපන් ස්ථානය වන ” වර්ණගර් “අතීතෙය්දී ෙබෞද්ධ අධ්‍යාපන කටයුතු පිළිබඳ ජාත්‍යන්තර මධ්‍යස්ථානයක් වුණා. කැණීම් මඟින් සිසුන් 2000ක් සඳහා වුණු ෙන්වාසිකාගාරයක් ෙසොයා ෙගන තිෙබනවා වාෙග්ම, ඒ මධ්‍යස්ථානය යළි සංවර්ධනය කිරීමට අප සැලසුම් කරනවා.

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, ෙසෞභාග්‍යමත් අනාගතයක් ඇති කර ගැනීම සඳහා අපෙග් රටවලට ආරක්ෂාව පිළිබඳ ශක්තිමත් අඩිතාලමක් වාෙග්ම කලාපය තුළ සාමය සහ ස්ථාවරත්වය පැවතීමත් අවශ්‍ය ෙවනවා. අප ෙදරෙටහි ආරක්ෂාව එකට බැඳී පවතිනවා. ඒ හා සමානවම, අපෙග් සමුදීය වටපිටාව සම්බන්ධෙයන් අප සතුව පවතින අෙන්‍යෝන්‍ය වගකීම ඉතා පැහැදිලියි. එකිෙනකාෙගන් ඉවත බලා සිටින්නට ෙනොහැකි වන ආකාරෙයන් ශී ලංකාව හා ඉන්දියාව ඉතා සමීපව පවතිනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම අප රටවල් එකිෙනකාෙගන් ෙවන් කරලා තබන එකත් කළ ෙනොහැක්කක් ෙවනවා. අප එක්ව පීඩාවන්ට මුහුණ ෙදන බව මෑත කාලීන ඉතිහාසය මඟින් ෙපන්වා දී තිෙබන අතර, අප ෙදරට එකිෙනකා හා එක්ව කටයුතු කිරීෙම්දී අපට වඩා සාධනීය ආකාරෙයන් කටයුතු කළ හැකියි. අපෙග් සහෙයෝගය 2004 වර්ෂෙය් සුනාමිය තුළින් ඇති වුණු අතිමහත් විනාශය සම්බන්ධෙයන් අවශ්‍ය කටයුතු කරෙගන යාමට අපට සහාය වුණා. මා මහ ඇමතිවරෙයක් වශෙයන් සිටියදී, 2001 වර්ෂෙය්දී ඇති වුණු භූජ්හි - Bhuj- භූමි කම්පාෙවන් පසුව සිදු කළ පතිසංස්කරණ කටයුතු සම්බන්ධ අපෙග් අත් දැකීම ෙබදා හදා ගැනීමට ලැබීම පිළිබඳ මා සතුටට පත් වුණා. අපෙග් සහෙයෝගය, තස්තවාදය හා අන්තවාදයට එෙරහිව සටන් කිරීම තුළින් අප ලත් සාර්ථකත්වය සඳහා වැදගත් සාධකයක් වුණා.

අප ෙදරට ඉදිරිෙය්ම ෙද්ශීය වශෙයන් ඇති වන තර්ජනයන් පවතිනවා. ඒවා නව ආකාරවලින් සහ නව මූලාශවලින් පැන නඟින තර්ජනයන් බව අප දකිනවා. තස්තවාදය ෙගෝලීයකරණය වීම අප ඉදිරිෙය් පැහැදිලිව පිළිඹිබු ෙවනවා. අප ෙදරට අතර සහෙයෝගීතාවය පිළිබඳ අවශ්‍යතාවය අන් කවරදාකටත් වඩා අද අත්‍යවශ්‍ය වී තිෙබනවා. අප ෙදරෙටහි ආරක්ෂාව සහ ෙසෞභාග්‍යය සඳහා ඉන්දියන් සාගරය ඉතාම වැදගත් ෙවනවා. ඒ වෙග්ම අප එක්ව කටයුතු කිරීම, විශ්වාසය හා අවංකභාවය මත පදනම් වූ වටපිටාවක් ෙගොඩ නඟා ගැනීම සහ එකිෙනකාෙග් අවශ්‍යතා පිළිබඳව සංෙව්දී අයුරින් කටයුතු කිරීම තුළින් අපෙග් ඉලක්ක හා අරමුණු සාක්ෂාත් කර ගැනීෙමහිලා අපට වඩාත් සාර්ථකව කටයුතු කළ හැකි ෙවනවා.

ශී ලංකාව සමඟ අප පවත්වන ආරක්ෂක සහෙයෝගීතාවය අපි අතිශයින්ම අගය කරනවා. ඉන්දියානු සාගර පෙද්ශෙය් අෙනකුත් රටවල් ඇතුළත් කර ගැනීම සඳහා අප විසින් ඉන්දියාව, ශී ලංකාව සහ මාල දිවයින අතර පවතින සමුද ආරක්ෂණ සහෙයෝගීතාවය වඩා ව්‍යාප්ත කළ යුතුයි.

21 වන ශතවර්ෂෙය් ගමන් මඟ තීරණය වනු ලබන්ෙන් ඉන්දියානු සාගරෙය් පවාහනය මත පදනම්ව බව මම නිතර පවසනවා. එහි දිශාව තීරණය කිරීම කලාපෙය් රටවල් සතුව පවතින වගකීමක්. අප ෙදරට ඉන්දියානු සාගරෙය් ඉතා වැදගත් සන්ධිස්ථානයක පිහිටා තිෙබන ෙදරටක් ෙවනවා. සාමකාමි, ආරක්ෂිත, තිරසාර සහ ෙසෞභාග්‍යමත් සමුදීය පටපිටාවක් නිර්මාණය කර ගැනීම සඳහා ඔබෙග් නායකත්වයත් අපෙග්

සහභාගීත්වයත් අතිශය වැදගත් ෙවනවා. ගැඹුරු අයුරින් එකෙනක සම්බන්ධ වී ඇති අපෙග් ජීවිතවල ෙවනස්කම් තිබීම ස්වාභාවිකයි. ඇතැම් විට එය සාමාන්‍ය මිනිසුන්ෙග් ජීවිතවලට බලපෑමක් ඇති කරනවා. ඒවා විසඳා ගැනීම සඳහා අපෙග් සංවාදය තුළ ඇති විවෘත බවත්, අපෙග් මානුෂීය හරයන්ෙග් ශක්තියත් ඒ සමඟම අපෙග් සම්බන්ධතාවෙය් කීර්තියත් අප සතුව පවතිනවා.

ගරු කථානායකතුමනි, ශී ලංකාව සහ ඉන්දියාව යන ෙදරට තම ජනතාවෙග් සිහින සැබෑ කර ගැනීම සඳහා වටිනා අවස්ථාවක් සහ වගකීමක් සහිත තත්ත්වයකට පත්ව සිටිනවා. ෙමය අපෙග් සම්බන්ධතා අලුත් කර ගැනීෙම් අවස්ථාවක් ෙවනවා ෙමන්ම අපෙග් හවුල්කාරීත්වෙයහි නව ආරම්භයක් ඇති කර ගැනීම සඳහා සහ නව ශක්තියක් ලබා දීම සඳහා වූ අවස්ථාවක් ෙවනවා. අප ෙදරට එකිෙනකට ආසන්නෙය් පිහිටීම සැමවිටම ෙදරට අතර සමීප බවකට පරිවර්තනය කර ගැනීමට අප වග බලාගත යුතුයි. පසුගිය මාසෙය්දී ජනාධිපති සිරිෙසේන මහතා තම පථම විෙදස් සංචාරය සඳහා ඉන්දියාව ෙතෝරා ගැනීම අපට මහත් ෙගෞරවයක් වුණා. ඒ වාෙග්ම ෙමරටට පැමිණි එතුමාෙග් පළමුවැනි අමුත්තා වීෙම් ෙගෞරවය ද මට ලැබුණා. අසල්වැසියන් අතර තිබිය යුත්ෙත් ෙමවැනි සම්බන්ධතාවයක් තමයි. ෙහට මම මඩු පාර දුම්රිය මාර්ගය විවෘත කිරීම සඳහා තෙලයිමන්නාරමට යනවා. ෙමය පැරණි ඉන්දියා-ශී ලංකා දුම්රිය මාර්ග සම්බන්ධතාවෙය් ෙකොටසක්. ෙශේෂ්ඨ ෙද්ශාභිමානී කවිෙයකු වූ සුභමනියන් භාරතී විසින් විසි වැනි සියවෙසේ මුල් භාගෙය්දී රචිත “සිංදු නදි යින් මීෙසයි” ගීතෙය් ෙප්ළි මට සිහිපත් ෙවනවා, ෙම් විධියට: “සිංහල තිවුනුක්ෙකෝර් පාලම් අෙමයිප්ෙපෝම්” - අපි ශී ලංකාවට පාලමක් හදමු.”

මම ඇවිත් ඉන්ෙන් ෙමම පාලම ෙගොඩ නැගීෙම් බලාෙපොෙරොත්තුව ඇතිවයි. ෙමය, අපි ෙදරටටම ෙපොදු උරුමය, අෙප් ෙපොදු වටිනාකම් හා දැක්ම, අෙප් අෙන්‍යෝන්‍ය සහෙයෝගය හා එක්සත්කම, මිතශීලී හුවමාරු කර ගැනීම්, ඵලදායී සහෙයෝගීතාවය සහ ඒ සියල්ලටමත් වඩා එකිෙනකා ෙකෙරහි ඇති විශ්වාසය හා අපට ෙපොදු ෛදවය යන ශක්තිමත් කුළුණු මත ඉදි ෙකෙරන පාලමක්.

ඔබ සැමට ස්තූතියි. ඔබ සමඟ එක්වීමට ලැබීම මට ලැබුණු ෙගෞරවයක්. නැවත වතාවක් ඔබට ස්තූතියි.

කථාෙව් ෙදමළ පරිවර්තනය

உைரயினᾐ தமிழ் ெமாழிெபயர்ப்ᾗ

TAMIL TRANSLATION OF THE SPEECH

பாராᾦமன்றத்தின் ெகௗரவ சபாநாயகர், ஸ்ரீமான் சமல் ராஜபக்ஷ ஜி, ெகௗரவ இலங்ைகப் பிரதம அைமச்சர் ஸ்ரீமான் ரணில் விக்கிரமசிங்க ஜி, ெகௗரவ எதிர்க் கட்சித் தைலவர் நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா, மற்ᾠம் ெகௗரவ பாராᾦமன்ற உᾠப்பினர்கேள, ெகௗரவ விᾞந்தினர்கேள, எழில், கலாசாரம் மற்ᾠம் நட்ᾗறᾫ ஆகியவற்றின் தாயகமாக விளங்கும் இலங்ைக விஜயத்ைதயிட்ᾌ மிக்க மகிழ்ச்சியைடகின்ேறன். இந்தப் பாராᾦமன்றத்தில் பிரசன்னமாக இᾞப்பைதயிட்ᾌ அதிக ெபᾞமிதம் ெகாள்கின்ேறன். அதன் ெசழிப்பான வரலாᾠ ெதாடர்பில் நன்கு அறிந்திᾞக்கின்ேறன். இந்தப் பாராᾦமன்றம் ஆசியாவின் மிகப் பழைமயான ஜனநாயகங்கᾦள் ஒன்ைறப் பிரதிநிதித்ᾐவம் ெசய்வேதாᾌ ெசயᾥக்கம் மிகுந்த ஒன்ைறᾜம் குறித்ᾐக்காட்ᾌகின்றᾐ. உலகத்தில் ேவᾠ பலைரᾜம்விட ᾙன்னராகேவ இலங்ைக ஒவ்ெவாᾞ தனிநபᾞக்கும் வாக்குாிைமையᾜம் ேபச்சுாிைமையᾜம் அளித்தᾐ.

இலங்ைக வாழ் மக்கᾦக்கு, ஆᾜேபாவன்! வணக்கம்! 1.25 பில்ᾢயன் நண்பர்களினᾐம் மில்ᾢயன் கணக்கான இலங்ைக கிாிக்ெகட் ஆதரவாளர்களினᾐம் வாழ்த்ᾐக்கைள ஏந்தி வந்ᾐள்ேளன். நான் ேபாத் கயா ேதசத்தின் நல்லாசிகைள அᾔராதᾗர ேதசத்ᾐக்குக் ெகாண்ᾌவᾞகின்ேறன். எம்மிைடேய பகிரப்பட்ᾌள்ள மரᾗகᾦக்கான உாிய மாியாைதᾜடᾔம் நாம் பகிர்ந்ᾐெகாண்ᾌள்ள எதிர்காலத்ᾐக்கான அர்ப்பணிப்ᾗடᾔம் இவ்விடத்தில் நின்ᾠ ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கின்ேறன். கடந்த ேம மாதத்தில் நான் பதவிப்பிரமாணம் ெசய்ᾐெகாண்ட ேவைளயில், அவ்ைவபவத்ᾐக்கான ெதற்காசியத் தைலவர்களின் பிரசன்னத்தினால் மிகᾫம் ெகௗரவிக்கப்பட்ேடன். எமᾐ பிராந்தியத்தில் ஜனநாயகத்தின் ᾙன்ேனாக்கிய நகர்ைவக் குறிக்கும் விழாவாகேவ அவர்களின் பிரசன்னம் அைமந்தᾐ. அேதேபால், எமᾐ ெபாᾐவான இலக்ைக அங்கீகாிக்கும் ெசயற்பாடாகᾫம் அᾐ காணப்பட்டᾐ. எந்தெவாᾞ நாட்ᾊனᾐம் எதிர்காலத்தில் அதன் அயல் நாᾌகளின் ஸ்திரநிைல ெசல்வாக்குச்

11 12

[ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමා]

2015 මාර්තු 13

ெசᾤத்ᾐகின்றᾐ என்ᾠ நம்ᾗகின்ேறன். இந்தியாவின் எதிர்காலத்ᾐக்காக நான் காᾎம் கனᾫதான் எமᾐ அயல் நாᾌகᾦக்காகᾫம் நான் விᾞம்ᾗம் எதிர்காலமாகும். இந்தப் பிராந்தியத்தில் நாம் ஒேர பயணத்ைத ேமற்ெகாண்ᾌள்ேளாம், எமᾐ மக்களின் வாழ்க்ைகைய மாற்றியைமப்பதற்கு.

நாம் அᾊேமல் அᾊ ைவத்ᾐ நகᾞம்ேபாᾐ எமᾐ பாைத இலகுவானதாகᾫம், பயணம் விைரவானதாகᾫம், குறிக்ேகாள் அண்மித்ததாகᾫம் அைமᾜம். நான் இப்ேபாᾐ ெகாᾨம்பில் நின்ᾠெகாண்ᾌ இமயத்ைத ேநாக்கி வடக்ேக பார்க்கும்ேபாᾐ, எமᾐ பிராந்தியத்தின் தனிச்சிறப்ைபᾜம் எமᾐ ெசல்வச் ெசழிப்பான பல்வைகைமையᾜம் ெபாᾐவான நாகாிகப் பிைணப்ᾗக்கைளᾜம் கண்ᾌ வியந்ᾐேபாகின்ேறன். நாம் ஒேர ᾚலத்தில் இᾞந்ᾐம் பின்னிப் பிைணந்ᾐள்ள வரலாற்றின் ஊடாகᾫம் உᾞவாக்கப்பட்ᾌள்ேளாம். இன்ᾠ, ெபᾞமிதம் ெகாண்ட, சுயாதீன ேதசங்களாக இைறைம மற்ᾠம் சமத்ᾐவத்ᾐடன் ஒன்றாக ைகேகார்த்ᾐள்ேளாம். இந்தியாᾫக்கும் இலங்ைகக்கும் நிலத்ெதாடர்ᾗ கிைடயாᾐ. ஆயிᾔம் அைனத்ᾐ விடயங்களிᾤம் நாம் மிக ெநᾞங்கிய அயலவர்களாகத் திகழ்கின்ேறாம். இந்தியாவிேலா இலங்ைகயிேலா எங்கு பார்த்தாᾤம், எமᾐ பிைணப்ᾗகளின் உட்கூᾠகளாகிய சமயங்கள், ெமாழிகள், கலாசாரங்கள், உணᾫகள், சடங்குகள், மரᾗகள், இதிகாசங்கள் என்பன ஆழ்ந்த, வᾤவான சிேநகத்ᾐடᾔம் நட்ᾗறᾫடᾔம் பாிணமிக்கின்றன. எம்மிைடேயயான உறᾫ மஹிந்த மற்ᾠம் சங்கமித்ரா ஆகிேயாாின் விஜயத்தின்ᾚலம் ெமᾞேகற்றப்பட்ᾌ வைரயᾠக்கப்பᾌகின்றᾐ. அவர்கள் இரண்டாயிரம் ஆண்ᾌகᾦக்கு ேமற்பட்ட காலத்ᾐக்கு ᾙன்னர், சமாதானம், சகிப்ᾗத்தன்ைம மற்ᾠம் நட்ᾗறᾫ ஆகியவற்றின் ெசய்திகைள ஏந்தி வந்தனர். தைலசிறந்த தமிழ்க் காவியமான சிலப்பதிகாரத்தின் ைமயக் கதாபாத்திரமாக விளங்கும் கண்ணகிைய இலங்ைகயில் பத்தினி ெதய்வமாக வழிபᾌவதிᾢᾞந்ᾐ இᾐ ெமய்ப்பித்ᾐக் காட்டப்பᾌகின்றᾐ; அᾐ இலங்ைகயில் இராமாயணத்தின் சுவᾌகளின் ஊடாகᾫம் நிைலத்ᾐநிற்கின்றᾐ; ேமᾤம் இᾐ நாகூர் ஆண்டவாின் தர்காவிᾤம் கிறிஸ்தவ ேதவாலயமான ேவளாங்கண்ணியிᾤம் பக்தி கலந்த உணர்ᾫடன் ெவளிப்பᾌகின்றᾐ; சுவாமி விேவகானந்தர், மற்ᾠம் இலங்ைகயிᾤம் இந்தியாவிᾤம் மகாேபாதி சங்கத்தின் தாபகரான அனகாாிக தர்மபால ஆகிேயாᾞக்கிைடயிலான நட்பிᾤம் இᾐ பிரதிபᾢப்பᾐடன், இந்தியாவிᾤம் இலங்ைகயிᾤம் உள்ள மகாத்மா காந்தியின் சீடர்களின் ெசயற்பாᾌகளின் ஊடாகᾫம் அᾐ உயிேராட்டமாக உள்ளᾐ. எல்லாவற்ᾠக்கும் ஆதர்சமாக, எம்மிைடேயயான உறᾫᾙைற சாமான்ய இந்தியர்கள் மற்ᾠம் இலங்ைகயர்களின் இரண்டறக் கலந்ᾐள்ள வாழ்க்ைக ᾙைறயின் ஊடாகᾫம் ெசழித்ேதாங்குகின்றᾐ. எமᾐ சுயாதீன வாழ்க்ைகᾙைற சமகாலத்தில் ெதாடங்கியைவ ஆகும். அப்ேபாதிᾞந்ᾐ இலங்ைக குறிப்பிடத்தக்க ᾙன்ேனற்றத்ைத அைடந்ᾐள்ளᾐ.

ேதசம் என்பᾐ எமᾐ பிராந்தியத்தில் மனித அபிவிᾞத்திக்கான அகத்ᾑண்ᾌதலாக அைமகின்றᾐ. இலங்ைக ெதாழில்ᾙயற்சி, ஆற்றல், தனிச்சிறப்பான ᾒண்மதிசார் மரᾗகள் ஆகியவற்றின் உைறவிடமாகத் திகழ்கின்றᾐ. உலகளாவிய தரம்வாய்ந்த வர்த்தகம் இங்ேக காணப்பᾌகின்றᾐ. இலங்ைக ெதற்காசியாவில் ஒத்ᾐைழப்ைப விᾞத்தி ெசய்வதில் தைலைமேயற்ᾠச் ெசயற்பᾌவேதாᾌ, இந்ᾐ சᾙத்திரப் பிராந்தியத்தின் எதிர்காலத்ᾐக்கு இᾐ ᾙக்கியத்ᾐவம் உைடயதாகᾫம் அைமகின்றᾐ. இலங்ைகயின் ᾙன்ேனற்றᾙம் சுபிட்சᾙம் இந்தியாவின் பலத்தின் ᾚலமாகᾫம் திகழ்கின்றன. எனேவ, இலங்ைகயின் ெவற்றி இந்தியாᾫக்கு அதிᾙக்கியத்ᾐவம் வாய்ந்ததாக அைமவேதாᾌ, நட்ᾗ நாᾌ என்ற ாீதியில் எமᾐ நல்வாழ்த்ᾐக்கள், எமᾐ ஆதரᾫ மற்ᾠம் ஒᾞைமப்பாᾌ என்பன எப்ேபாᾐம் இலங்ைகᾜடன் இᾞந்ᾐள்ளன. அவ்வாேற அைவ எப்ேபாᾐம் உங்கᾦக்குக் கிைடக்கும். எமᾐ பிராந்தியத்திᾤள்ள எம் அைனவாினᾐம் ெவற்றி, ேதசம் என்ற ாீதியில் எம்ைம நாம் எவ்வாᾠ வைரயᾠத்ᾐக் ெகாள்கின்ேறாம் என்பதில்தான் தங்கிᾜள்ளᾐ. இப்பிராந்தியத்தில் உள்ள நாம் அைனவᾞம், உண்ைமயில் பல்வைகைம ெகாண்ட ஒவ்ெவாᾞ ேதசᾙம், எமᾐ சᾙதாயங்களின் பல்ேவᾠ பிாிᾫகᾦக்கான அைடயாளப்பᾌத்தல் மற்ᾠம் உட்பᾌத்தல், உாிைமகள், ேகாாிக்ைககள், சுய ெகௗரவம் மற்ᾠம் வாய்ப்ᾗ ேபான்ற பிரச்சிைனகᾦக்கு ᾙகம்ெகாᾌத்ᾐ வந்ᾐள்ேளாம். நாம் ᾐயரம் மிகுந்த வன்ᾙைறக்கு ᾙகம்ெகாᾌத்ᾐள்ேளாம்; நாம் ெகாᾍர பயங்கரவாதத்ᾐடன் ேபாராᾊᾜள்ேளாம்; அவ்வாேற, சுᾙகமான தீர்ᾫகளின் ெவற்றிகரமான ᾙன்ᾔதாரணங்கைளᾜம் கண்ᾌள்ேளாம். நாம் ஒவ்ெவாᾞவᾞம் இ்ந்தச் சிக்கலான பிரச்சிைனகைள எமக்ேக உாிய பாணியில் தீர்த்ᾐக்ெகாள்ள ᾙைனந்ᾐள்ேளாம். எனிᾔம், நல்ᾢணக்கத்ைத ஏற்பᾌத்ᾐவேத எமᾐ ேதர்வாக அைமந்தᾐ. எனக்கு ஒᾞ விடயம் ெவளிப்பைடயாகத் ெதாிகின்றᾐ: பல்வைகைம ேதசங்களின் பலத்ᾐக்கான ேதாற்ᾠவாயாக அைமய ᾙᾊᾜம்.

எமᾐ சᾙதாயத்தின் அைனத்ᾐப் பிாிவினர்களினᾐம் அபிலாைசகᾦக்கு நாம் இடமளிக்கும்ேபாᾐ, ஒவ்ெவாᾞ தனிநபாினᾐம் பலம் ேதசத்ᾐக்குக் கிட்ᾌகின்றᾐ. ேமᾤம், நாம் மாநிலங்கள், மாவட்டங்கள் மற்ᾠம் கிராமங்கᾦக்கு வᾤᾬட்ᾌம்ேபாᾐ எமᾐ நாட்ைட ேமᾤம் ேமᾤம் பலப்பᾌத்திக்ெகாள்கின்ேறாம். இதைன நீங்கள் எனᾐ பக்கச்சார்ᾗ

என்ᾠகூட அைழக்கலாம். நான் 13 வᾞடங்களாக ᾙதலைமச்சராகᾫம் பிரதம அைமச்சராக, ஒᾞ வᾞடத்திᾤம் குைறவான காலப்பகுதியிᾤம் கைடைமயாற்றிᾜள்ேளன்.

இன்ᾠ, இந்தியாவிᾤள்ள மாநிலங்கைளப் பலப்பᾌத்ᾐவேத எனᾐ தைலயாய ᾙன்ᾔாிைமயாகக் காணப்பᾌகின்றᾐ. நான் கூட்ᾊைணவான சமஷ்ᾊ ᾙைறைமயில் உᾠதியான நம்பிக்ைக ெகாண்ᾌள்ேளன். எனேவ, நாங்கள் மாநிலங்கᾦக்கு ேமᾤம் அதிகாரத்ைதᾜம் வளங்கைளᾜம் பகிர்ந்தளிப்பேதாᾌ, ேதசிய தீர்மானங்கைள ேமற்ெகாள்ᾦம் நைடᾙைறகளில் அவர்கைளᾜம் ᾙைறசார் பங்காளிகளாக இைணத்ᾐக் ெகாள்கின்ேறாம்.

இலங்ைக தசாப்தகால அவல வன்ᾙைற மற்ᾠம் சர்ச்ைசகைளக் கடந்ᾐ வந்ᾐள்ளᾐ. நீங்கள் ெவற்றிகரமாகப் பயங்கரவாதத்ைத ேதாற்கᾊத்ᾐ, ேமாதைல ᾙᾊᾫக்குக் ெகாண்ᾌவந்ᾐள்ளீர்கள். சᾙதாயத்தின் அைனத்ᾐ பிாிவினாினᾐம் மனங்கைள ெவல்வதற்கான, காயங்கைள ஆற்ᾠவதற்கான வரலாற்ᾠ ாீதியில் வாய்ப்பான இத்தᾞணத்தில் நீங்கள் நின்ᾠ ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கின்றீர்கள். அண்ைமயில் இலங்ைகயில் நைடெபற்ற ேதர்தல் ேதசத்தின் ஏேகாபித்த குரைல, மாற்றம், நல்ᾢணக்கம், ஒற்ᾠைம ஆகியவற்ᾠக்கான எதிர்பார்ப்ைபப் பிரதிபᾢத்தᾐ. நீங்கள் அண்ைமக் காலங்களில் ேமற்ெகாண்ட நடவᾊக்ைககள் ᾐணிகரமானைவᾜம் வியக்கத்தக்கைவᾜம் ஆகும். அைவ ᾗதிய ஆரம்பத்ைதக் குறித்ᾐ நிற்கின்றன.

ஒவ்ெவாᾞவᾞக்கும் ஒற்ᾠைம மற்ᾠம் ஒᾞைமப்பாᾌ, சமாதானம் மற்ᾠம் நல்ᾢணக்கம், வாய்ப்ᾗ மற்ᾠம் கண்ணியம் ஆகியவற்றினால் இலங்ைகயின் எதிர்காலம் நிர்ணயிக்கப்பᾌவᾐ ெதாடர்பில் நான் உᾠதியான நம்பிக்ைக உைடயவன். அைத எய்ᾐவதில் இலங்ைக ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கும் ஆற்றைல நான் நம்ᾗகின்ேறன். அᾐ எமᾐ ெபாᾐவான நாகாிக மரᾗாிைமகளின் அᾊப்பைடயில் அைமந்ᾐள்ளᾐ. ᾙன்ேனாக்கிᾜள்ள பாைத இலங்ைக ேமற்ெகாள்ளேவண்ᾊᾜள்ள ெதாிவாகும். அᾐ நாட்ᾊᾤள்ள சᾙதாயத்தின் சகல பிாிᾫகளினᾐம் சகல அரசியல் அறிஞர்களினᾐம் கூட்ᾌப் ெபாᾠப்பாகும். ஆயிᾔம், இந்தியாவிற்கு, இலங்ைகயின் ஒற்ᾠைம மற்ᾠம் ஒᾞைமப்பாᾌ என்பன இன்றியைமயாதனவாகும் என்பைத என்னால் உᾠதியாகக் கூறᾙᾊᾜம். அᾐ எமᾐ அக்கைறயில் ேவᾟன்றிᾜள்ளᾐ. இந்தக் ேகாட்பாட்ᾊᾤள்ள எமᾐ ெசாந்த அᾊப்பைட நம்பிக்ைககளிᾢᾞந்ᾐ அᾐ ேதாற்றம் ெபᾠகின்றᾐ.

ெகௗரவ சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, மதிப்ᾗக்குாிய உᾠப்பினர்கேள, எனᾐ ேநாக்கின் பிரகாரம் ᾙᾨைமயான சுற்ᾠப்ᾗறம் என்பᾐ, பிராந்தியத்தில் உள்ள பங்காண்ைமகள் நைடᾙைற ஒᾨங்கின் இலகுபᾌத்தᾤடன் உᾞவாக்கப்பᾌகின்றேபாᾐ, வணிகம், ᾙதலீᾌகள், ெதாழில்ᾒட்பம், கᾞத்ᾐகள் மற்ᾠம் மக்கள் இலகுவாக எல்ைலகைளக் கடந்ᾐ ெசல்ᾤம் ஒன்றாகும்.

இந்தியாவில் வளர்ச்சிேவகம் இயல்ᾗநிைலக்குக் ெகாண்ᾌவரப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ. உலகில் மிகத்ᾐாிதமாக வளர்ந்ᾐவᾞம் பாாிய ெபாᾞளாதாரமாக இந்தியா மாறிᾜள்ளᾐ. ெபாᾞளாதார வாய்ப்ᾗக்குாிய ᾗதியெதாᾞ தளமாக உலகம் இந்தியாைவ ேநாக்குகிறᾐ. ஆனாᾤம், இந்தியாவின் மீதான ᾙதலாவᾐ உாிைமக் ேகாாிக்ைக எமᾐ அயலவர்கᾦக்ேக, இலங்ைகக்ேக உாியதாகும் என்பைத நான் மீண்ᾌம் கூᾠகின்ேறன். எமᾐ அயலவர்களின் ᾙன்ேனற்றத்தில் இந்தியா ஓர் ஊக்கியாகத் ெதாழிற்பᾊன், நான் மகிழ்ச்சியைடேவன். எமᾐ பிராந்தியத்தில், மிகப் பலம்வாய்ந்த ெபாᾞளாதார பங்குதாரராகத் திகழ்வதற்கான ஆற்றல் இலங்ைகயிடம் உண்ᾌ. வர்த்தகத்ைத அதிகாித்ᾐ அைத ேமᾤம் சமநிைலப்பᾌத்ᾐவதற்காக, உங்கᾦைடய அக்கைறகள் ெதாடர்பான நடவᾊக்ைககைள ேமற்ெகாள்வதற்கு நாம் உங்கᾦடன் பணியாற்ᾠேவாம். இந்தியாவின் வர்த்தகச் சூழல் ேமᾤம் ேமᾤம் மிகᾫம் திறந்ததாக மாறிவᾞகின்றᾐ. இந்த ேபாட்ᾊத் தன்ைமயான உலகில் இலங்ைக ஏைனயைவகᾦடன் பின்தங்கிவிடக்கூடாᾐ. அதனால்தான் நாம் குறிக்ேகாள்மிக்க, பரந்ᾐபட்ட ெபாᾞளாதார பங்குைடைம உடன்பᾊக்ைக (CEPA) ஒன்ைற ஏற்பᾌத்தேவண்ᾌம். இந்தியா மற்ᾠம் ஏைனய நாᾌகᾦக்கான ஏற்ᾠமதிக்கும் உங்களᾐ உட்கட்டைமப்ைபக் கட்ᾊெயᾨப்ᾗவதற்குமான ᾙதலீᾌகளின் ஓர் இயற்ைகத் ேதாற்ᾠவாயாகᾫம் இந்தியா அைமயலாம். நாங்கள் இன்ᾠ சிறந்த ᾙன்ேனற்றத்ைத அைடந்ᾐள்ேளாம். எனேவ, சᾙத்திரப் ெபாᾞளாதாரத்தின் மிகப்ெபாிய ᾚல வாய்ப்ᾗவளத்ைதப் பயன்பᾌத்திக்ெகாள்வதற்காக ஒன்றிைணந்ᾐ பணிᾗாிேவாம்.

ெதற்காசியப் பிராந்தியத்திᾤம் அதᾔடன் இைணந்த பல்ᾐைற ெதாழில்ᾒட்ப மற்ᾠம் ெபாᾞளாதார ஒத்ᾐைழப்ᾗக்கான வங்களா விாிகுடா ᾙன்ெனᾌப்ᾗப் (BIMSTEC) பிராந்தியத்திᾤம் ஒத்ᾐைழப்ைப அதிகாிப்பதில்

13 14

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

இரண்ᾌ நாᾌகᾦம் ᾙன்னிைல வகிக்கேவண்ᾌம். இந்தப் பாாிய பிராந்தியத்ைத நிலம் மற்ᾠம் கடல் ஆகியவற்றினால் இைணக்கும் எமᾐ இரண்ᾌ நாᾌகᾦம் பிராந்திய சுபிட்சத்தின் ெபாறிகளாகத் திகழᾙᾊᾜம். இலங்ைகᾜடனான பங்குைடைமைய ேமம்பᾌத்ᾐவதற்காக இந்தியா ᾙᾨைமயான அர்ப்பணிப்ைப ேமற்ெகாள்ᾦம் என்பைத என்னால் உᾠதியாகக் கூறᾙᾊᾜம். ஒᾞ நண்பாின் அல்லᾐ அயலவாின் ெபாᾠப்பாகேவ நாங்கள் இதைனக் கᾞᾐகின்ேறாம். இந்தியா அபிவிᾞத்திக்கான உதவியாக 1.6 பில்ᾢயன் அெமாிக்க ெடாலர்கைள வழங்குகின்றᾐ. இன்ᾠ ᾗைகயிரத ᾐைறக்காக ேமலதிக உதவியாக 318 மில்ᾢயன் அெமாிக்க ெடாலர்கைள வழங்குவதற்கு உᾠதியளித்ᾐள்ேளாம். நாம் எமᾐ அபிவிᾞத்திப் பங்குைடைமையத் ெதாடᾞேவாம். நாங்கள் உங்களᾐ அரசாங்கத்தினால் வழிநடத்தப்பᾌேவாம். அத்ᾐடன், நாங்கள் எமᾐ ெசாந்த நாட்ᾊல் எதிர்பார்க்கும் ெவளிப்பைடத்தன்ைமயின் அேதயளᾫ மட்டத்தில் பணிᾗாிேவாம். கடந்த மாதம் நாங்கள் அᾎசக்தியின் சாத்ᾪகப் பிரேயாகங்கள் பற்றிய ஒத்ᾐைழப்ᾗ மீதான உடன்பᾊக்ைகெயான்றில் ைகச்சாத்திட்ᾌள்ேளாம். பிராந்தியத்தின் ேவᾠ எந்தப் பகுதிையᾜம்விட, விவசாயம், கல்வி, சுகாதாரம், விஞ்ஞானம் மற்ᾠம் ெதாழில்ᾒட்பம், விண்ெவளி ஆகிய ᾐைறகளில் இலங்ைகᾜடன் ஒத்ᾐைழப்ைப விாிᾫபᾌத்ᾐவதற்கான அதிகளᾫ வாய்ப்ᾗ வளங்கைள நான் காண்கிேறன்.

உண்ைமயில், நாங்கள் எமᾐ கற்பைனயினால் மட்ᾌேம கட்ᾌப்பᾌத்தப்பட்ᾌள்ேளாம். சார்க் பிராந்தியத்ᾐக்கான இந்திய ெசய்மதியின் ᾙᾨைமயான பயைன இலங்ைக ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ᾦம் என நாங்கள் நம்ᾗகிேறாம். 2016 ᾊசம்பாில் அᾐ விண்ெவளியில் இᾞக்கும். எமᾐ உறᾫ ᾙைறயின் இதயமாக மக்கள் உள்ளனர். நாம் மக்கைள இைணக்கும்ெபாᾨᾐ, ேதசியங்கᾦக்கிைடயிலான பிைணப்ᾗம் பலம் அைடகிறᾐ. இதனால்தான் வᾞைகயின்ேபாதான ᾪசா வசதிைய இலங்ைகப் பிரைசகᾦக்கு விஸ்தாிக்க நாம் தீர்மானித்ேதாம். எங்கள் நாᾌகᾦக்கிைடயிலான ெதாடர்ைபᾜம் நாம் அதிகாிப்ேபாம். எமᾐ கலாசார, மத பிைணப்ᾗகைளப் பலப்பᾌத்ᾐேவாம். ெடல்ᾢயிᾤள்ள ேதசிய அᾞம்ெபாᾞளகத்தில் கபிலவஸ்த்ᾐப் ᾗனித சின்னங்கைள பார்ைவயிᾌவதற்கு வᾞைகதᾞம் இலங்ைகயர்கᾦக்கான கட்டணக் குைறப்ைபக் கடந்த மாதம் நாம் அறிவித்ேதாம். ஒᾞ கண்காட்சி ஊடாக எமᾐ பகிரப்பட்ட ெபளத்த பாரம்பாியத்ைத உங்கᾦக்கு அண்ைமயாகக் ெகாண்ᾌவᾞேவாம். எமᾐ ெபளத்த, இராமாயண சுவᾌகைள நாம் ஒன்றாக விᾞத்தி ெசய்ேவாம். எனᾐ பிறப்பிடமான வர்ணகார், ᾗராதன காலத்தில் ெபளத்த கற்ைகக்கான ஒᾞ சர்வேதச நிைலயமாக விளங்கியᾐ. 2,000 மாணவர்கᾦக்கான விᾌதிெயான்ᾠ அகழ்வாராய்ச்சிகளின்ேபாᾐ கண்ᾌபிᾊக்கப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐடன், நிைலயத்ைத மீள்விᾞத்தி ெசய்வதற்கான திட்டங்கᾦம் ேமற்ெகாள்ளப்பᾌகின்றன.

ெகளரவ சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, எமᾐ நாᾌகᾦக்கான பாᾐகாப்பின் பலமான ஓர் அத்திபாரத்ைதᾜம் பிராந்தியத்தில் அைமதிையᾜம் ஸ்திரத் தன்ைமையᾜம் எதிர்கால சுபிட்சம் ேவண்ᾊநிற்கின்றᾐ. எமᾐ இᾞ நாᾌகளினᾐம் பாᾐகாப்ᾗ, ஒன்றிᾢᾞந்ᾐ ஒன்ᾠ பிாிக்க ᾙᾊயாதᾐ. அᾐேபாலேவ எமᾐ கடல்சார் சுற்ᾠப்ᾗறம் மீதான எமᾐ பகிரப்பட்ட ெபாᾠப்ᾗம் ெதளிவானᾐ. இந்தியாᾫம் இலங்ைகᾜம் ஒன்ைறெயான்ᾠ பார்க்க மிகᾫம் ெநᾞக்கமானைவேய அல்லாமல், ஒன்றிᾢᾞந்ᾐ மற்றைத ெதாடர்பᾠக்கᾫம் ᾙᾊயாᾐ. எமᾐ அண்ைமக்கால வரலாᾠகள் நாம் ஒன்றாகத் ᾐன்பப்பட்டைதக் காட்ᾌகின்றன. நாம் ஒᾞவேராெடாᾞவர் ேசர்ந்ᾐ பணியாற்ᾠம்ேபாᾐ மிகᾫம் விைனத்திறᾔடன் இᾞந்ேதாம். 2004ஆம் ஆண்ᾊன் சுனாமி அழிᾫகள் ெதாடர்பான நடவᾊக்ைககளில் எமᾐ ஒத்ᾐைழப்ᾗ உதவியᾐ. 2001இல் ‘ᾘச்’ நிலநᾌக்கத்திற்குப் பின்னர் ஒᾞ ᾙதலைமச்சர் என்ற வைகயில் ᾗனரைமப்பில் எமᾐ அᾔபவத்ைதப் பகிர்ந்ᾐெகாள்வதில் மகிழ்ச்சியைடந்ேதன். பயங்கரவாதம் மற்ᾠம் தீவிரவாதத்ᾐடன் ேபாராᾌவதில் எமᾐ ெவற்றிக்கு, எமᾐ ஒத்ᾐைழப்ᾗ அவசியமாக இᾞந்தᾐ.

எம் இᾞ நாᾌகளிᾤம் உள்நாட்ᾌ அச்சுᾠத்தல்கள் உள்ளன. அச்சுᾠத்தல்கள் ᾗதிய வᾊவங்களிᾤம் ᾗதிய ᾚலங்களிᾢᾞந்ᾐம் எᾨவைத நாம் காண்கின்ேறாம். பயங்கரவாதம் உலகமயமாவைத நாம் காண்கின்ேறாம். எமᾐ ஒத்ᾐைழப்ᾗக்கான ேதைவ எப்ெபாᾨைதᾜம்விட இன்ᾠ மிகᾫம் அத்தியாவசியமானதாக உள்ளᾐ. இᾞ நாᾌகளினᾐம் பாᾐகாப்ᾗக்கும் ெசழிப்ᾗக்கும் இந்ᾐ சᾙத்திரம் ᾙக்கியமானᾐ. நாம் இைணந்ᾐ ெசயலாற்ᾠவᾐடன், நம்பிக்ைக, விசுவாசம்மிக்க சூழைலக் கட்ᾊெயᾨப்பி ஒᾞவர் மற்றவாின் விᾞப்ᾗகᾦக்கு கூᾞணர்வாக இᾞப்பின், இந்த இலக்குகைள அைடவதில் ெவற்றியைடயᾙᾊᾜம். இலங்ைகᾜடனான எமᾐ பாᾐகாப்ᾗ ஒத்ᾐைழப்ைப நாம் ஆழமாக மதிக்கின்ேறாம். இந்தியா, இலங்ைக மற்ᾠம் மாைலதீᾫக்கு இைடயிᾤம் இந்ᾐ சᾙத்திரப் பகுதியிᾤள்ள ஏைனய நாᾌகைளᾜம் உள்ளடக்கி அவற்ᾠக்கிைடயில் கடல்சார் பாᾐகாப்ᾗ ஒத்ᾐைழப்ைப நாம் விஸ்தாிக்க ேவண்ᾌம்.

இந்ᾐ சᾙத்திரத்தின் நீேராட்டங்களினாேலேய 21ஆம் ᾓற்றாண்ᾊன் ெசல்வழி தீர்மானிக்கப்பᾌம் என நான் அᾊக்கᾊ கூᾠேவன். அதன் திைசைய நிர்ணயிப்பᾐ பிராந்தியத்திᾤள்ள நாᾌகளின் ெபாᾠப்பாகும். இந்ᾐ சᾙத்திரத்தின் சந்தியிᾤள்ள இᾞ நாᾌகளாக நாம் உள்ேளாம். உங்களᾐ தைலைமத்ᾐவᾙம் எங்களᾐ பங்காண்ைமᾜம் ஓர் அைமதியானᾐம் பாᾐகாப்பானᾐம் ஸ்திரமானᾐம் வளமானᾐமான கடல்சார் சுற்ᾠப்ᾗறத்ைதக் கட்ᾊெயᾨப்ᾗவதற்கு ᾙக்கியமானᾐ. எமᾐ ஆழமாக ஒன்றிைணக்கப்பட்ட வாழ்வில் ேவᾠபாᾌகைளக் ெகாண்ᾊᾞப்பᾐ இயல்பானᾐ. சிலேவைளகளில் இᾐ சாதாரண மக்களின் வாழ்ைவத் ெதாᾌகிறᾐ. அவற்ைறத் தீர்ப்பதற்கு எமᾐ உைரயாடᾢன் ெவளிப்பைடத்தன்ைமᾜம் மனித விᾨமியங்களில் பலᾙம் உறᾫᾙைறயில் நல்ெலண்ணᾙம் எம்மிடம் உள்ளன.

ெகௗரவ சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, எமᾐ மக்களின் கனᾫகைள நனவாக்க இலங்ைகᾜம் இந்தியாᾫம் ஒᾞ சிறந்த சந்தர்ப்பத்ைதᾜம் ெபாᾠப்ைபᾜம் ெகாண்ட தᾞணம் ஒன்றில் இᾞக்கிறᾐ. எமᾐ உறᾫகைளப் ᾗᾐப்பித்ᾐ எமᾐ பங்குைடைமயில் ᾗதியெதாᾞ ெதாடக்கத்ைதᾜம் ᾪாியத்ைதᾜம் ஏற்பᾌத்ᾐவதற்கான ேநரᾙம் இᾐவாகும். ᾗவியியல் ாீதியாக நாம் அண்மித்திᾞப்பᾐ எப்ேபாᾐம் எமக்கிைடயிலான ெநᾞக்கத்தன்ைமயாகப் பாிணமிப்பைத நாம் உᾠதி ெசய்ய ேவண்ᾌம். சனாதிபதி ைமத்திாிபால சிறிேசன கடந்த மாதம் தனᾐ ᾙதலாவᾐ விஜயத்திற்கான இடமாக இந்தியாைவத் ேதர்ந்ெதᾌத்தைம எமக்குக் கிைடத்த ெகளரவமாகும். இங்கு அவரᾐ ᾙதல் விᾞந்தாளியாக நான் இᾞப்பᾐம் ெகளரவமாக உள்ளᾐ. அயலவர்கᾦக்கிைடேயயான உறᾫ இவ்வாᾠ தான் இᾞத்தல் ேவண்ᾌம். மᾌ பிரேதசத்ᾐக்கான ᾗைகயிரதச் ேசைவைய ஆரம்பித்ᾐ ைவப்பதற்கு நான் நாைள தைலமன்னார் ெசல்ேவன். இᾐ பைழய இந்திய-இலங்ைக ᾗைகயிரத இைணப்பின் அங்கமாகும். 20ஆம் ᾓற்றாண்ᾊன் ஆரம்பத்தில் ேதசியவாதப் ᾗலவர் சுப்பிரமணிய பாரதியார் இயற்றிய “சிந்ᾐ நதியின் மிைச” என்ற ᾗகழ்ெபற்ற பாடᾢன் “சிங்களத் தீவிᾔக்ேகார் பாலம் அைமப்ேபாம்” – நாங்கள் இலங்ைகக்கு ஒᾞ பாலம் அைமப்ேபாம் என்ᾔம் வாிகள் எனᾐ நிைனவிற்கு வᾞகின்றன.

நமᾐ பகிரப்பட்ட மரᾗாிைம, பகிரப்பட்ட விᾨமியங்கள் மற்ᾠம் ேநாக்கு பரஸ்பர ஆதரᾫ மற்ᾠம் ஒற்ᾠைம சிேனகᾘர்வ பாிமாற்றங்கள் மற்ᾠம் ஆக்கᾘர்வ ஒத்ᾐைழப்ᾗ மற்ᾠம் இைவ அைனத்ᾐக்கும் ேமலாக ஒᾞவᾞக்ெகாᾞவர் மீதான நம்பிக்ைக மற்ᾠம் பகிரப்பட்ட நமᾐ விதி ஆகிய உᾠதியான ᾑண்கள் தாங்கியிᾞக்கும் இந்தப் பாலத்ைதக் கட்ᾊெயᾨப்ᾗம் எதிர்பார்ப்ᾗடன் நான் இங்கு வந்ᾐள்ேளன்.

நன்றி, உங்கᾦடன் இᾞக்கக்கிைடத்தைம ஒᾞ ெகௗரவமாகும். மீண்ᾌம் ஒᾞᾙைற எனᾐ நன்றிைய உங்கᾦக்குத் ெதாிவிக்கிேறன் . කථානායකතුමා (சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (Mr. Speaker) Thank you very much, Your Excellency. The Vote of Thanks is to be delivered by the Hon. Prime Minister.

ගරු රනිල් විකමසිංහ මහතා (අගාමාත්‍යතුමා සහ පතිපත්ති සම්පාදන, ආර්ථික කටයුතු, ළමා, තරුණ හා සංස්කෘතික කටයුතු අමාත්‍යතුමා) (மாண்ᾗமிகு ரணில் விக்கிரமசிங்க - பிரதம அைமச்சᾞம் ெகாள்ைக உᾞவாக்கம், ெபாᾞளாதார அᾤவல்கள், சிᾠவர், இைளஞர் மற்ᾠம் கலாசார அᾤவல்கள் அைமச்சᾞம்) (The Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe - Prime Minister, Minister of Policy Planning, Economic Affairs, Child, Youth and Cultural Affairs) Hon. Speaker, it gives us great pleasure to have in this House and to address us, Shri Narendra Modi, Prime Minister of India. It is a visit, I might say, that was long overdue and you, Sir, have fulfilled it starting a new chapter and a closer relationship between our two nations. You described our Parliament as being vibrant. I must tell Shri Narendra Modi that is an understatement and at the moment you are seeing it in its more subdued hour. But, that is the essence of democracy.

15 16

[ඉන්දීය අගාමාත්‍ය අතිගරු ශී නෙර්න්ද ෙමෝදි මැතිතුමා]

2015 මාර්තු 13

We have the oldest Parliament in Asia. Our history goes back to the Legislative Council of 1835 and, we have here today in this House the Hon. D.M. Swaminathan, the Minister of Resettlement, Reconstruction and Hindu Religious Affairs, a descendant of one of its original Members, the late Hon. Arumugampillai Coomaraswami. You traced our history of the universal franchise and of a Westminster System. But, as you rightly said, it is not only the Westminster System. The world forgets that the history of popular assemblies is not confined to Greece. It is much older - from the Republics of the Ganges Plain, the Litcchavi Republics to whom the Gautama Buddha preached that "as long as you meet in harmony; as long as you discuss in harmony; as long as you depart in harmony, a country cannot go into decay" and that is what we ourselves are trying to achieve today in Sri Lanka. How do we move from a Westminster tradition towards a more cooperative culture while keeping the identities of political parties and the natural struggle for power, which would come in a democracy during the election time? But, our traditions are not confined merely to the Litcchavians or, as we all know very well, the bringing of the doctrine of the Gautama Buddha by Venerable Mahinda Thero.

We are actually a successor to the Mauryan Tradition, a tradition which lived in Sri Lanka through the Anuradhapura and the Polonnaruwa Kingdoms, long after it ceased to be so in India. We developed our ruling systems, our cities, our culture and even our language of the Sinhalese, which is based on Pali. All this is part of our Mauryan heritage, to which we added a hydraulic civilization unparalleled in this region. But, Hon. Prime Minister, it has not been a one-way journey. The original Tamil Kingdom was established with the help of a Sinhala Prince of Anuradhapura - Prince Manawamma - who commanded one of the armies of Narasimhavarman, the King of Pallava, who defeated Pulakesin and Chalukyan Kingdom to establish the first Tamilian Kingdom in South India. Sri Lanka had a relationship with the Pallava Kingdom and with Kanchipuram, as the last centre of Buddhism. In close collaboration with the Pandayan and then together with the Pandayan and Sri Wijaya, we dominated the Indian Ocean and the Bay of Bengal until the Cholas defeated all of us and became the ruling power.

So, we have been a part and parcel of that history, a history which had actually been even brought closer by a modern Sri Lanka; a modern India, the two countries which also inherited not only our past but also the language of English, the traditions of the supremacy of law, of Legislature, of Cabinet Government and more recently, that of cricket. We are, in fact, two sides of the same coin, travelling on a same journey of peace and prosperity for our people and security for the region. We have a common destiny. As you pointed out, we were the richest region in the world till the 16th Century. Now, we

have to achieve that again. Indo-Lanka relations again will be the foundation stone of converting our region back into prosperity, as you yourself emphasized in your speech.

It should also be based on trade and I must thank you for granting the on-arrival visas, the e-visas, which will be a starting point. You have given us a thought-provoking speech and it is certainly a valuable contribution to the process that we have to start from here. We are also happy to see - I must say - an Indian Government which is focusing and giving priority to a policy orientation on its neighbours and the Indian Ocean Region. The success of this will lie on how we give a new life to SAARC, making it a platform for the political leaders of the region to exchange ideas and to give new life to the Indian Ocean Region, and in that, I would like to say to Shri Narendra Modi, India has the leading role to play and the responsibility. We too have our own role and together we can do this journey.

So, what you have given to us is the opening where we can transform the lives of our people and of the region and on behalf of this House, let me say thank you for all the assistance and also for opening a new chapter for close cooperation between our two countries.

Thank you.

ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා (විරුද්ධ පාර්ශ්වෙය් නායකතුමා) (மாண்ᾗமிகு நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா - எதிர்க்கட்சி ᾙதல்வர்) (The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva - Leader of the Opposition) Your Excellency Shri Narendra Modi, Prime Minister of India, Hon. Speaker of Parliament, Hon. Prime Minister of Sri Lanka, Hon. Ministers, Hon. Members of Parliament and Distinguished Invitees. As the Leader of the Opposition, I feel honoured and privileged to propose the Vote of Thanks on Your Excellency’s historic visit to the Parliament of Sri Lanka and let me take this opportunity to express my profound appreciation and thanks to Your Excellency for the honour bestowed upon this House with your presence here today.

Your visit to Sri Lanka heralds a new era of renewed Indo-Lanka relations. Sri Lanka and India have a long history of close ties socially, politically, culturally and economically spanning over many centuries. Religious scriptures tell us that Lord Buddha, the great philosopher and the esteemed son of the Maha Bharath visited Sri Lanka several times and shared his knowledge with us and blessed our Motherland. History records that King Asoka’s son and daughter and his disciples brought Buddhism and the order of Maha-Sangha to Sri Lanka, 2500 years ago guiding our ancestors on a religious and spiritual path transforming Sri Lanka into a disciplined society.

17 18

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

Bodh Gaya, Varanasi, Kapilavastu and many places of religious worship in India are visited by hundreds of thousands of devout Sri Lankan Buddhists annually, bringing India and its people closer to the hearts and minds of our people. Puttaparthi, Tirupati, Whitefield and Velankanni are some other places of religious worship frequented by Sri Lankans of other religious denominations as well as Buddhists. Similarly, many Indians too visit popular religious places in Sri Lanka, such as Kataragama and Seetha Eliya, which has further strengthened the ties between the two nations.

Many Indian leaders have visited Sri Lanka in the past strengthening bilateral economic cooperation and improving our cultural and social ties in the past. From time immemorial, Sri Lanka and India have had excellent trade relations and as a result, we are proud that India has become one of our leading trading partners.

Your Excellency, you are a self-made man worthy of emulation, and you are a glowing example to all our politicians in Sri Lanka and also the SAARC Region. Without a family dynasty to back you, your inspiring journey to the office of the Prime Minister of Maha Bharath, starting from very humble beginnings in Vadnagar, a rural town in North Gujarat, has been a journey of courage, compassion and constant hard work devoting your entire life to the service of your people. I believe, the secret of your great success is your simplicity, dedication and determination coupled with a disciplined life-style winning the hearts and minds of your people.

Your 13-year long stint as the Chief Minister of Gujarat ushered a paradigm shift towards a pro-people and a pro-active good governance to make it work efficiently, honestly and humanely. You have transformed Gujarat which was reeling after a devastating earthquake, into a vibrant growth-engine contributing strongly to India’s development. As the former Minister of Irrigation and Water Resources Management, I had the opportunity of visiting Gujarat to personally witness these spectacular changes you have made to this State to improve its infrastructure, lift irrigation and agriculture. I witnessed how the Narmada River waters were very effectively and efficiently diverted through lift irrigation to provide safe drinking water to 30 million people and irrigate 560,000 hectares of water-starved land using innovative Indian Technology demonstrating your great vision.

As a result of your dynamism, dedication and determination you were able to obtain an absolute majority in Lok Sabha for your party to form a very stable Government which was only a distant dream for the

previous governments of India. As a result, the stability so created has influenced not only India but the region as a whole.

Let me conclude, thanking Your Excellency once again for your inspiring speech to our Parliamentarians and for being here with us today. I am sure your visit will further strengthen our bilateral relations and friendship between the two nations.

May the Triple Gem bless you and protect you always! Ham Aapke Lambe Aur Swasth Jeevan Aur Swarnim Bhavishya Ki Kamna Karthe Hain. Dhanyawath.

We wish you a long and healthy life and a golden future.

Thank you.

කථානායකතුමා (சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (Mr. Speaker) Thank you, Hon. Prime Minister and Hon. Leader of the Opposition. Now, I wish to invite all the distinguished guests to the Members’ Dining Room and all the Members of Parliament to the Lobby for refreshments immediately after the Adjournment of the House.

Thank you.

කල්තැබීම ஒத்திைவப்ᾗ ADJOURNMENT ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (වැවිලි කර්මාන්ත අමාත්‍ය සහ පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුෙව් සභානායකතුමා) (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல - ெபᾞந்ேதாட்டக் ைகத்ெதாழில் அைமச்சᾞம் பாராᾦமன்றச் சைப ᾙதல்வᾞம்) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella - Minister of Plantation Industries and Leader of the House of Parliament)

Sir, I move,

“That the Parliament do now adjourn”. පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ඊට අනුකූලව අ. භා. 4.05ට, 2015 මාර්තු 17 වන අඟහරුවාදා අ. භා 1.00 වන ෙතක් කල් ගිෙය්ය.

அதன்பᾊ பி. ப. 4.05 மணிக்கு பாராᾦமன்றம், 2015 மார்ச் 17, ெசவ்வாய்க்கிழைம பி. ப. 1.00 மணிவைர ஒத்திைவக்கப்பட்டᾐ.

Adjourned accordingly at 4.05 p.m. until 1.00 p.m. on Tuesday, 17th March, 2015.

[ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා]

සැ.යු. ෙමම වාර්තාෙව් අවසාන මුදණය සඳහා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුතු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්තීන් මින් පිටපතක් ෙගන නිවැරදි කළ යුතු ආකාරය එහි පැහැදිලිව ලකුණු ෙකොට, පිටපත ලැබී ෙදසතියක් ෙනොඉක්මවා හැන්සාඩ් සංස්කාරක ෙවත ලැෙබන ෙසේ එවිය යුතුය.

குறிப்ᾗ உᾠப்பினர் இᾠதிப் பதிப்பிற் ெசய்யவிᾞம்ᾗம் பிைழ திᾞத்தங்கைளத் தமᾐ பிரதியில் ெதளிவாகக் குறித்ᾐ அதைனப் பிைழ

திᾞத்தப்படாத பிரதி கிைடத்த இᾞ வாரங்கᾦள் ஹன்சாட் பதிப்பாசிாியᾞக்கு அᾔப்ᾗதல் ேவண்ᾌம். හැන්සාඩ් වාර්තා ෙකොළඹ 5 කිරුළපන මාවෙත් රජෙය් පවෘත්ති ෙදපාර්තෙම්න්තුෙව් පිහිටි රජෙය් පකාශන කාර්යාංශෙයන් මිල දී ගත හැක.

ஹன்சாட் பிரதிகைள ெகாᾨம்ᾗ 5, கிᾞலப்பைன மாவத்ைதயிᾤள்ள அரசாங்க தகவல் திைணக்களத்தின்

அரசாங்க ெவளியீᾌகள் அᾤவலகத்தில் பணம் ெசᾤத்திப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளலாம். Hansard Reports can be purchased from the Government Publications Bureau at the Department of Government Informa-tion, Kirulapone Avenue, Colombo 5.
